margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">根据15号公告第一条规定，原《附列资料（一）》中的第4a栏调整为第3栏，项目名称由“10%税率的货物及加工修理修配劳务”调整为“9%税率的货物及加工修理修配劳务”，第4b栏调整为第4栏，项目名称由“10%税率的服务、不动产和无形资产”调整为“9%税率的服务、不动产和无形资产”，因此开具的税率为9%的增值税专用发票、增值税普通发票列明的金额、税额应填写在“9%税率的货物及加工修理修配劳务”“9%税率的服务、不动产和无形资产”的对应栏次。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本行“开具增值税专用发票”“销售额”列=200000（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本行“开具增值税专用发票”“销项(应纳)税额”列=18000（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">该企业2019年4月（税款所属期）《附列资料（一）》填报如下所示：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2.该企业2019年4月（税款所属期）主表填报如下所示：</p></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section><p><img src=\"/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190509/1557366653228717.png\" title=\"1557366653228717.png\" alt=\"202.png\"/></p><p><br/></p><p><br/></p><p><br/></p><section><section><section><section><section><section><section><h1 style=\"font-size: 32px; font-weight: bold; border-bottom-color: rgb(204, 204, 204); border-bottom-width: 2px; border-bottom-style: solid; padding: 0px 4px 0px 0px; text-align: left; margin: 0px 0px 10px;\">案例3：开具16%税率红字发票申报表填写</h1><p><br/></p></section><section></section><section></section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><p>某企业为增值税一般纳税人，2019年6月发生2019年2月销售的货物退货，开具一张16%税率的红字增值税专用发票，金额40000元，税额6400元；销售一批商品，开具一张13%税率的增值税专用发票，金额60000元，税额7800元。<br/></p><section><section><section><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0.3em 0.5em; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; word-wrap: break-word !important; display: inline-block; border-radius: 0.5em; font-size: 14px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background-color: rgb(40, 187, 181);\"><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">分析</p></span></section><section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; word-wrap: break-word !important; font-size: 14px;\">根据15号公告第一条规定，原《附列资料（一）》中的第1栏项目名称由“16%税率的货物及加工修理修配劳务”调整为“13%税率的货物及加工修理修配劳务”，因此开具的税率为13%的增值税专用发票列明的金额、税额应填写在“13%税率的货物及加工修理修配劳务”的对应栏次。根据15号公告第三条“本公告施行后，纳税人申报适用16%、10%等原增值税税率应税项目时，按照申报表调整前后的对应关系，分别填写相关栏次”规定，因此该企业开具的16%税率红字专用发票，应填写在“13%税率的货物及加工修理修配劳务”栏次。</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; word-wrap: break-word !important; font-size: 14px;\">1.《附列资料（一）》第1行“13%税率的货物及加工修理修配劳务”：</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; word-wrap: break-word !important; font-size: 14px;\">本行“开具增值税专用发票”“销售额”列=-40000+60000=20000（元）</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; word-wrap: break-word !important; font-size: 14px;\">本行“开具增值税专用发票”“销项（应纳）税额”列=-6400+7800=1400（元）</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; word-wrap: break-word !important; font-size: 14px;\">该企业2019年6月（税款所属期）《附列资料（一）》填报如下所示：</span></p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><img src=\"/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190509/1557366634501227.png\" title=\"1557366634501227.png\" alt=\"301.png\"/></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2.该企业2019年6月（税款所属期）主表填报如下所示：</p></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><p><img src=\"/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190509/1557366626995012.png\" title=\"1557366626995012.png\" alt=\"302.png\"/></p><p><br/></p></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section><section><h1 style=\"font-size: 32px; font-weight: bold; border-bottom-color: rgb(204, 204, 204); border-bottom-width: 2px; border-bottom-style: solid; padding: 0px 4px 0px 0px; text-align: left; margin: 0px 0px 10px;\">案例4：不动产进项税额抵扣申报表填写</h1><p><br/></p></section><section></section><section></section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">某企业为增值税一般纳税人，2019年6月购进不动产，取得1份增值税专用发票并已认证相符，金额8000000元，税额720000元。</p></section></section></section><section><section><section><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0.3em 0.5em; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; word-wrap: break-word !important; display: inline-block; border-radius: 0.5em; font-size: 14px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background-color: rgb(40, 187, 181);\"><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">分析</p></span></section><section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">根据39号公告规定，自2019年4月1日起，《营业税改征增值税试点有关事项的规定》（财税〔2016〕36号印发）第一条第（四）项第1点、第二条第（一）项第1点停止执行，纳税人取得不动产或者不动产在建工程的进项税额不再分2年抵扣。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">该纳税人取得的购入不动产的增值税专用发票所列进项税额应填入《增值税纳税申报表附列资料（二）》（本期进项税额明细，以下称《附列资料（二）》）对应栏次，同时填入本表第9栏“（三）本期用于购建不动产的扣税凭证”。</p><ol class=\" list-paddingleft-2\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\"><li><section><section><section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">该企业2019年6月（税款所属期）《附列资料（二）》填报如下所示：</p></section></section></section></section></section></section></li></ol><p><img src=\"/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190509/1557366581427712.png\" title=\"1557366581427712.png\" alt=\"401.png\"/></p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2.该企业2019年6月（税款所属期）主表填报如下所示：</p></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img src=\"/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190509/1557366574100186.png\" title=\"1557366574100186.png\" alt=\"402.png\"/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section><section><h1 style=\"font-size: 32px; font-weight: bold; border-bottom-color: rgb(204, 204, 204); border-bottom-width: 2px; border-bottom-style: solid; padding: 0px 4px 0px 0px; text-align: left; margin: 0px 0px 10px;\">案例5：不动产待抵扣进项税额抵扣申报表填写</h1><p><br/></p></section><section></section><section></section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">某企业为增值税一般纳税人，2019年3月税款所属期，《增值税纳税申报表附列资料（五）》（不动产分期抵扣计算表）第6栏“期末待抵扣不动产进项税额”的期末余额为450000元。2019年5月税款所属期，企业决定将未抵扣的税额进行抵扣。</p></section></section></section><section><section><section><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0.3em 0.5em; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; word-wrap: break-word !important; display: inline-block; border-radius: 0.5em; font-size: 14px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background-color: rgb(40, 187, 181);\"><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">分析</p></span></section><section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">按照政策规定2019年4月1日起，《营业税改征增值税试点有关事项的规定》（财税〔2016〕36号印发）第一条第（四）项第1点、第二条第（一）项第1点停止执行，纳税人取得不动产或者不动产在建工程的进项税额不再分2年抵扣。此前按照上述规定尚未抵扣完毕的待抵扣进项税额，可自2019年4月税款所属期起从销项税额中一次性抵扣，结转填入《附列资料（二）》第8b栏“其他”。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">1.该企业2019年5月（税款所属期）《附列资料（二）》填报如下所示：</p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><img src=\"/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190509/1557366496726359.png\" title=\"1557366496726359.png\" alt=\"501.png\"/></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2.该企业2019年5月（税款所属期）主表填报如下所示：</p></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><img src=\"/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190509/1557366490988701.png\" title=\"1557366490988701.png\" alt=\"502.png\"/></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section><section><h1 style=\"font-size: 32px; font-weight: bold; border-bottom-color: rgb(204, 204, 204); border-bottom-width: 2px; border-bottom-style: solid; padding: 0px 4px 0px 0px; text-align: left; margin: 0px 0px 10px;\">案例6：旅客运输服务进项税额抵扣申报表填写</h1><p><br/></p></section><section></section><section></section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">某企业为增值税一般纳税人，2019年4月购进按规定允许抵扣的国内旅客运输服务。取得1份增值税专用发票，金额20000元，税额1800元；取得1份增值税电子普通发票，金额8000元，税额720元；取得1张注明旅客身份信息的航空运输电子客票行程单，票价2200元，民航发展基金50元，燃油附加费120元；取得5张注明旅客身份信息的铁路车票，票面金额合计2180元；取得15张注明旅客身份信息的公路、水路等其他客票，票面金额合计5150元。</p></section></section></section><section><section><section><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0.3em 0.5em; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; word-wrap: break-word !important; display: inline-block; border-radius: 0.5em; font-size: 14px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background-color: rgb(40, 187, 181);\"><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">分析</p></span></section><section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">根据39号公告第六条规定，纳税人购进国内旅客运输服务，其进项税额允许从销项税额中抵扣。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">取得增值税专用发票的，可抵扣的进项税额为发票上注明的税额，即1800元；</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">取得增值税电子普通发票的，可抵扣进项税额为发票上注明的税额，即720元；</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">取得注明旅客身份信息的航空运输电子客票行程单的，按照下列公式计算进项税额：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">航空旅客运输进项税额=（票价+燃油附加费）÷（1+9%）×9%=（2200+120）÷（1+9%）×9%=191.56（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">需要注意，民航发展基金不作为计算进项税额的基数。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">取得注明旅客身份信息的铁路车票的，按照下列公式计算进项税额：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">铁路旅客运输进项税额=票面金额÷（1+9%）×9%=2180÷（1+9%）×9%=180（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">取得注明旅客身份信息的公路、水路等其他客票的，按照下列公式计算进项税额：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">公路、水路等其他旅客运输进项税额=票面金额÷（1+3%）×3%=5150÷（1+3%）×3%=150（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">1.《附列资料（二）》第2行“其中：本期认证相符且本期申报抵扣”：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本行“份数”列=1（份）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本行“金额”列=20000（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本行“税额”列=1800（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">《附列资料（二）》第8b行“其他”：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本行“份数”列=22（份）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本行“金额”列=8000+（2200+120）÷（1+9%）+2180÷（1+9%）+5150÷（1+3%）=17128.44（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本行“税额”列=720+191.56+180+150=1241.56（元），本行填写企业取得的除增值税专用发票以外的其他扣税凭证允许抵扣的进项税额。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">《附列资料（二）》第10行“（四）本期用于抵扣的旅客运输服务扣税凭证”：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本行“份数”列=23（份）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本行“金额”列=20000+17128.44=37128.44</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本行“税额”列=1800+1241.56=3041.56（元），本行填写企业本月允许抵扣的所有国内旅客运输服务进项税额。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">该企业2019年4月（税款所属期）《附列资料（二）》填报如下所示：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img src=\"/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190509/1557366435289958.png\" title=\"1557366435289958.png\" alt=\"601.png\"/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">（2）该企业2019年4月（税款所属期）主表填报如下所示：</p></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><p><img src=\"/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190509/1557366445900664.png\" title=\"1557366445900664.png\" alt=\"602.png\"/></p><p><br/></p></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section><section><h1 style=\"font-size: 32px; font-weight: bold; border-bottom-color: rgb(204, 204, 204); border-bottom-width: 2px; border-bottom-style: solid; padding: 0px 4px 0px 0px; text-align: left; margin: 0px 0px 10px;\">案例7：适用加计抵减政策申报表填写</h1><p><br/></p></section><section></section><section></section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">某企业2018年3月20日成立，自2019年1月1日起登记为一般纳税人。在2018年4月至2018年12月小规模期间，仅提供信息技术服务取得销售额400000元，2019年1月至2019年3月一般纳税人期间，提供信息技术服务取得销售额580000元，销售应税货物取得销售额200000元。企业2019年4月，发生销项税额50000元，取得一般计税项目进项税额100000元。</p></section></section></section><section><section><section><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0.3em 0.5em; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; word-wrap: break-word !important; display: inline-block; border-radius: 0.5em; font-size: 14px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background-color: rgb(40, 187, 181);\"><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">分析</p></span></section><section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">根据39号公告第七条第一项规定，自2019年4月1日至2021年12月31日，允许生产、生活性服务业纳税人按照当期可抵扣进项税额加计10%，抵减应纳税额（以下称加计抵减政策）。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本公告所称生产、生活性服务业纳税人，是指提供邮政服务、电信服务、现代服务、生活服务（以下称四项服务）取得的销售额占全部销售额的比重超过50%的纳税人。四项服务的具体范围按照《销售服务、无形资产、不动产注释》（财税〔2016〕36号印发）执行。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2019年3月31日前设立的纳税人，自2018年4月至2019年3月期间的销售额(经营期不满12个月的，按照实际经营期的销售额)符合上述规定条件的，自2019年4月1日起适用加计抵减政策。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">该企业在2018年4月至2019年3月期间，提供现代服务取得销售额占全部销售额比重=（400000+580000）÷（400000+580000+200000）=83%，超过50%，适用加计抵减政策。需要注意的是，在计算销售额比重时，应包含小规模期间发生的销售额。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">1.情景一：如企业于2019年4月通过电子税务局（或前往办税服务厅）提交《适用加计抵减政策的声明》，确认适用政策有效期为2019年4月1日至2019年12月31日。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">企业2019年4月可计提的加计抵减额=100000×10%=10000（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">按照15号公告规定，企业计提的加计抵减额应填写在《增值税纳税申报表附列资料（四）》（税额抵减情况表，以下称《附列资料（四）》）相关栏次。由于该企业2019年4月销项税额小于进项税额，本期应纳税额为0，所以计提的加计抵减额不应在本期抵减，应填写在《附列资料（四）》第6行“期末余额”列，留待下期抵减。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">（1）该企业2019年4月（税款所属期）《附列资料（四）》填报如下所示：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img src=\"/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190509/1557366379335368.png\" title=\"1557366379335368.png\" alt=\"701.png\"/></p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2.该企业2019年4月（税款所属期）《增值税纳税申报表（一般纳税人适用）》（以下称主表）填报如下所示：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img src=\"/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190509/1557366796466823.png\" title=\"1557366796466823.png\" alt=\"702.png\"/></p></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">该企业2019年4月销项税额小于进项税额，应纳税额为0元。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2.情景二：如企业于2019年6月通过电子税务局（或前往办税服务厅）提交《适用加计抵减政策的声明》，按照39号公告相关规定，适用政策有效期应为2019年4月至2019年12月。企业2019年5月取得的进项税额为120000元，期末留抵税额为0元，2019年6月取得的进项税额为80000元，2019年6月发生的销项税额为160000元。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">纳税人可计提但未计提的加计抵减额，可在确定适用加计抵减政策当期一并计提。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">（1）企业2019年6月可计提的加计抵减额=（100000+120000+80000）×10%=30000（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">该企业2019年6月（税款所属期）《附列资料（四）》填报如下所示：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img src=\"/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190509/1557366361219215.png\" title=\"1557366361219215.png\" alt=\"703.png\"/></p></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">（2）按照15号公告附件2《增值税纳税申报表（一般纳税人适用）》及其附列资料填写说明的规定，适用加计抵减政策的纳税人，应纳税额按以下公式填写：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本栏“一般项目”列“本月数”＝第11栏“销项税额”“一般项目”列“本月数”-第18栏“实际抵扣税额”“一般项目”列“本月数”-“实际抵减额”；</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本栏“即征即退项目”列“本月数”＝第11栏“销项税额”“即征即退项目”列“本月数”-第18栏“实际抵扣税额”“即征即退项目”列“本月数”-“实际抵减额”。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">该企业2019年6月应纳税额=本期销项税额-本期进项税额-本期实际抵减额=160000-80000-30000=50000（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">该企业2019年6月（税款所属期）主表填报如下所示：</p></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><img src=\"/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190509/1557366349684125.png\" title=\"1557366349684125.png\" alt=\"704.png\"/></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">需注意主表第19行“应纳税额”等于主表第11行-主表第18行-《附列资料（四）》第6行本期实际抵减额。</p></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section><section><h1 style=\"font-size: 32px; font-weight: bold; border-bottom-color: rgb(204, 204, 204); border-bottom-width: 2px; border-bottom-style: solid; padding: 0px 4px 0px 0px; text-align: left; margin: 0px 0px 10px;\">案例8：适用加计抵减政策申报表填写</h1><p><br/></p></section><section></section><section></section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">某企业2019年5月1日成立，自2019年5月1日起登记为一般纳税人。在2019年5月至2019年7月期间，提供信息技术服务取得销售额600000元，销售货物取得销售额400000元，抵扣的进项税额合计为60000元，2019年7月期末留抵税额为0元。该企业2019年8月发生销项税额100000元，取得进项税额50000元。</p></section></section></section><section><section><section><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0.3em 0.5em; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; word-wrap: break-word !important; display: inline-block; border-radius: 0.5em; font-size: 14px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background-color: rgb(40, 187, 181);\"><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">分析</p></span></section><section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">根据39号公告第七条第一项规定，自2019年4月1日至2021年12月31日，允许生产、生活性服务业纳税人按照当期可抵扣进项税额加计10%，抵减应纳税额（以下称加计抵减政策）。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本公告所称生产、生活性服务业纳税人，是指提供邮政服务、电信服务、现代服务、生活服务（以下称四项服务）取得的销售额占全部销售额的比重超过50%的纳税人。四项服务的具体范围按照《销售服务、无形资产、不动产注释》（财税〔2016〕36号印发）执行。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2019年4月1日后设立的纳税人，自设立之日起3个月的销售额符合上述规定条件的，自登记为一般纳税人之日起适用加计抵减政策。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">该企业在2019年5月至2019年7月期间，提供现代服务取得销售额占全部销售额比重=600000÷（600000+400000）=60%，超过50%，适用加计抵减政策。企业可于2019年8月通过电子税务局（或前往办税服务厅）提交《适用加计抵减政策的声明》，确认适用政策有效期为2019年5月至2019年12月。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">按照39号公告相关规定，纳税人可计提但未计提的加计抵减额，可在确定适用加计抵减政策当期一并计提。该企业2019年5月至2019年7月已抵扣的进项税额可以在2019年8月一并计提加计抵减额。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">1.企业2019年8月可计提的加计抵减额=（60000+50000）×10%=11000（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">该企业2019年8月（税款所属期）《附列资料（四）》填报如下所示：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"white-space: normal; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img src=\"http://www.kuaiqitong.com/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190509/1557366256598518.png\" title=\"1557366256598518.png\" alt=\"801.png\"/></strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2.按照15号公告附件2《增值税纳税申报表（一般纳税人适用）》及其附列资料填写说明的规定，适用加计抵减政策的纳税人，应纳税额按以下公式填写：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本栏“一般项目”列“本月数”＝第11栏“销项税额”“一般项目”列“本月数”-第18栏“实际抵扣税额”“一般项目”列“本月数”-“实际抵减额”；</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本栏“即征即退项目”列“本月数”＝第11栏“销项税额”“即征即退项目”列“本月数”-第18栏“实际抵扣税额”“即征即退项目”列“本月数”-“实际抵减额”。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">企业2019年8月应纳税额=本期销项税额-本期进项税额-本期实际抵减额=100000-50000-11000=39000（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">该企业2019年8月（税款所属期）主表填报如下所示：</p></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><img src=\"/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190509/1557366253226958.png\" title=\"1557366253226958.png\" alt=\"802.png\"/></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">需注意主表第19行“应纳税额”等于主表第11行-主表第18行-《附列资料（四）》第6行的本期实际抵减额。</p></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section><section><h1 style=\"font-size: 32px; font-weight: bold; border-bottom-color: rgb(204, 204, 204); border-bottom-width: 2px; border-bottom-style: solid; padding: 0px 4px 0px 0px; text-align: left; margin: 0px 0px 10px;\">案例9：适用加计抵减政策申报表填写</h1><p><br/></p></section><section></section><section></section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">某企业为增值税一般纳税人，2019年6月增值税申报表《附列资料（四）》第六行“一般项目加计抵减额计算”期末余额为5000元，2019年7月需要转出的进项税额60000元，该部分进项税额前期已计提加计抵减额。</p></section></section></section><section><section><section><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0.3em 0.5em; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; word-wrap: break-word !important; display: inline-block; border-radius: 0.5em; font-size: 14px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background-color: rgb(40, 187, 181);\"><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">分析</p></span></section><section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">根据39号公告第七条第二项规定，已计提加计抵减额的进项税额，按规定作进项税额转出的，应在进项税额转出当期，相应调减加计抵减额。计算公式如下：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">当期计提加计抵减额=当期可抵扣进项税额×10%</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">当期可抵减加计抵减额=上期末加计抵减额余额+当期计提加计抵减额-当期调减加计抵减额</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">1.该企业2019年7月（税款所属期）《附列资料（二）》填报如下所示：</p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><img src=\"/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190509/1557366202668715.png\" title=\"1557366202668715.png\" alt=\"901.png\"/></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2.该企业2019年7月当期调减加计抵减额=当期进项税额转出额×10%=60000×10%=6000（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">该企业2019年7月本期可抵减额=期初余额+本期发生额-本期调减额=5000+0-6000=-1000（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">该企业2019年7月（税款所属期）《附列资料（四）》填报如下所示：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img src=\"/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190509/1557366192384527.png\" title=\"1557366192384527.png\" alt=\"902.png\"/></p></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">需注意，本期可抵减额为负数时，本期实际抵减额为0，《附列资料（四）》中期末余额为-1000，留待下期冲减即可，不形成本期应纳税额。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">3.该企业7月本期应纳税额=销项税额-实际抵扣税额=0-（-60000）=60000（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">该企业2019年7月（税款所属期）主表填报如下所示：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img src=\"/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190509/1557366180989598.png\" title=\"1557366180989598.png\" alt=\"903.png\"/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section><section><h1 style=\"font-size: 32px; font-weight: bold; border-bottom-color: rgb(204, 204, 204); border-bottom-width: 2px; border-bottom-style: solid; padding: 0px 4px 0px 0px; text-align: left; margin: 0px 0px 10px;\">案例10：期末留抵税额退税后申报表填写</h1><p><br/></p></section><section></section><section></section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">某企业为增值税一般纳税人，2019年3月税款所属期“期末留抵税额”为100000元，2019年4月至2019年9月税款所属期“期末留抵税额”均大于100000元，2019年9月税款所属期“期末留抵税额”为700000元；该企业符合增值税期末留抵税额退税政策，2019年10月征期内向主管税务机关申请退还留抵税额，进项构成比例为80%，主管税务机关于当月批准并退还留抵税额288000元，企业于2019年10月30日取得退还的留抵税额。</p></section></section></section><section><section><section><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0.3em 0.5em; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; word-wrap: break-word !important; display: inline-block; border-radius: 0.5em; font-size: 14px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background-color: rgb(40, 187, 181);\"><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">分析</p></span></section><section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">根据39号公告第八条第（六）项，自2019年4月1日起，试行增值税期末留抵税额退税制度。纳税人取得退还的留抵税额后，应相应调减当期留抵税额。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">允许退还的增量留抵税额=增量留抵税额×进项构成比例×60%=（700000-100000）×80%×60%=288000（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">主管税务机关于2019年10月退还留抵税额288000元，因此纳税人应在2019年10月（税款所属期）申报时，将退还的留抵税额288000元填入《附列资料（二）》第22栏“上期留抵税额退税”。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">1.该企业2019年10月（税款所属期）《附列资料（二）》的填报如下所示：</p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><img src=\"/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190509/1557366087124286.png\" title=\"1557366087124286.png\" alt=\"101.png\"/></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2.该企业2019年10月（税款所属期）主表填报如下所示：</p></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><img src=\"/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190509/1557366078286198.png\" title=\"1557366078286198.png\" alt=\"102.png\"/></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section><section><h1 style=\"font-size: 32px; font-weight: bold; border-bottom-color: rgb(204, 204, 204); border-bottom-width: 2px; border-bottom-style: solid; padding: 0px 4px 0px 0px; text-align: left; margin: 0px 0px 10px;\">案例11：综合申报表填写</h1><p><br/></p></section><section></section><section></section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">某企业为增值税一般纳税人，2019年4月发生有形动产经营租赁业务，开具4张13%税率的增值税专用发票，金额合计1200000元，税额合计156000元；销售应税货物，开具1张13%税率的增值税普通发票，金额80000元，税额10400元。购进按规定允许抵扣的国内旅客运输服务，取得1张增值税专用发票，金额50000元，税额4500元；取得1张注明旅客身份信息的航空运输电子客票行程单，票价2000元，民航发展基金50元，燃油附加费120元；取得5张注明旅客身份信息的公路、水路等其他客票，票面金额合计2060元。购进一栋不动产，取得1张增值税专用发票，金额1500000元，税额135000元。企业2019年4月符合加计抵减政策，并已通过电子税务局提交《适用加计抵减政策的声明》。</p></section></section></section><section><section><section><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0.3em 0.5em; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; word-wrap: break-word !important; display: inline-block; border-radius: 0.5em; font-size: 14px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background-color: rgb(40, 187, 181);\"><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">分析</p></span></section><section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本期销项税额=156000+10400=166400（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">购进国内旅客运输服务取得增值税专用发票的，可抵扣的进项税额为发票上注明的税额，即4500元；</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">取得注明旅客身份信息的航空运输电子客票行程单的，按照下列公式计算进项税额：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">航空旅客运输进项税额=（票价+燃油附加费）÷（1+9%）×9%=（2000+120）÷（1+9%）×9%=175.05（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">需要注意，民航发展基金不作为计算进项税额的基数。</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">取得注明旅客身份信息的公路、水路等其他客票的，按照下列公式计算进项税额：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">公路、水路等其他旅客运输进项税额=票面金额÷（1+3%）×3%=2060÷（1+3%）×3%=60（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">购进国内旅客运输服务进项税额合计=4500+175.05+60=4735.05（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">购进不动产取得增值税专用发票的，可抵扣的进项税额为发票上注明的税额，即135000元；</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本期可抵扣进项税额=4735.05+135000=139735.05（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">企业2019年4月可计提的加计抵减额=139735.05×10%=13973.51（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本期应纳税额=本期销项税额-本期进项税额-本期实际抵减额=166400-139735.05-13973.51=12691.44（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">1.《附列资料（一）》第1行“13%税率的货物及加工修理修配劳务”：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本行“开具其他发票”“销售额”列=80000（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本行“开具其他发票”“销项(应纳)税额”列=10400（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">《附列资料（一）》第2行“13%税率的服务、不动产和无形资产”：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本行“开具增值税专用发票”“销售额”列=1200000（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本行“开具增值税专用发票”“销项(应纳)税额”列=156000（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本月销项(应纳)税额合计=156000+10400=166400（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">该企业2019年4月（税款所属期）《附列资料（一）》填报如下所示：</p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><section><section><section></section></section></section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><img src=\"/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190509/1557366022964292.png\" title=\"1557366022964292.png\" alt=\"1101.png\"/></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2.《附列资料（二）》第2行“其中：本期认证相符且本期申报抵扣”：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本行“份数”列=2（份）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本行“金额”列=50000+1500000=1550000（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">本行“税额”列=4500+135000=139500（元）</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; clear: both; min-height: 1em; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">《附列资料（二）》第8b行“其他”：</p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">1、非正常状态期间增值税、消费税和相关附加需补办的申报均为零申报的；</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2、非正常状态期间企业所得税月（季）度预缴需补办的申报均为零申报，且不存在弥补前期亏损情况的。</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">（二）</span><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">纳税人办理税务注销前，无需向税务机关提出终止“委托扣款协议书”申请。税务机关办结税务注销后，委托扣款协议自动终止</span><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">。</span></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">三、进一步减少证件、资料报送</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">三、未办理过涉税事宜的纳税人，若需要取得清税文书的，如何办理税务注销？</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">根据149号文第一条规定，</span><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">未办理过涉税事宜的纳税人若符合市场监管部门简易注销条件，可以直接向市场监管部门申请办理简易注销登记，免予到税务机关办理清税证明。</span><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">实践中还有一些未办理过涉税事宜的纳税人主动到税务机关办理清税，要求取得清税文书。为进一步优化纳税服务，响应纳税人诉求，《通知》规定这类纳税人主动到税务机关清税的，税务机关即时出具清税文书。</span><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">具体做法是，纳税人持加载统一社会信用代码的营业执照到注册地税务机关办理，税务机关即时出具清税文书。</span></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">四、办理过涉税事宜，但未领用过发票的纳税人如何办理税务注销？</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">一是对无欠税（滞纳金）及罚款、资料齐全的纳税人，税务机关即时出具清税文书。</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">二是对无欠税（滞纳金）及罚款、资料不齐（包括未办结事项要求报送的资料不齐）的，可采取“承诺制”容缺办理。</span><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">例如，纳税人需要报送的财务报表资料、纳税申报资料、有多缴税款需要提交退还多缴税款资料等，如果纳税人不能及时提供这些资料但急需清税文书的，可先作出承诺，税务机关即时出具清税文书，纳税人应按承诺的时限补齐资料并办结相关事项。纳税人若未履行承诺的，按照149号文规定，税务机关将对其法定代表人、财务负责人纳入纳税信用D级管理。</span></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">三是符合市场监管部门简易注销条件的纳税人，也可以按149号文规定，</span><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">直接向市场监管部门申请办理简易注销登记，免予到税务机关办理清税证明。</span></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">五、办理过涉税事宜，且领用过发票的纳税人如何办理税务注销？</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">此类纳税人办理税务注销仍按现有规定执行。其中，符合149号文第二条规定条件的纳税人，可享受税务注销即办服务。</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">六、依法破产的纳税人如何办理税务注销？</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">此类纳税人可持人民法院出具的终结破产程序裁定书向税务机关申请办理税务注销，税务机关即时出具清税文书。对于纳税人仍存在的欠税，税务机关按照规定进行“死欠”核销处理。</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">七、拟注销的纳税人申请解除非正常管理状态，税务机关如何简化补办申报手续？</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">为提高办税效率，对于非正常状态期间未开展生产经营活动、无相关纳税义务的纳税人，《通知》增加了批量零申报相关规定。具体做法是，税务机关打印《批量零申报确认表》，纳税人确认后，对相关税（费）种进行批量零申报处理。批量零申报涉及的相关税（费）种具体包括：企业所得税月（季）度预缴申报、增值税和消费税以及相关附加税（费）。</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">八、纳税人办理税务注销前，“委托扣款协议书”如何终止？</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">九、《通知》减少了哪些报送资料？</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">1.《税务登记证》正（副）本、《临时税务登记证》正（副）本和《发票领用簿》。</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">十、《通知》从什么时候开始实施？</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2019年7月1日施行</span><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;
