margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">那么，现在企业注销到底该怎么操作呢？</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; text-align: left; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; font-size: 16px; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(188, 37, 39); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2019年</strong></span><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; color: rgb(188, 37, 39);\">注销公司的相关流程</strong></span></p><section><section><section><section></section></section></section></section></section><section><br/></section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">在政府的扶持政策下，工商注册流程越来越简单化，新设立的企业也越来越多，但是也有很多企业经营不下去，不了了之，今天给大家总结注销公司的相关流程以及注意事项：</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">一、公司注销的条件</span></strong></span></p></section></section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">1、公司被依法宣告破产；&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2、公司章程规定营业期限届满或者其他解散事由出现；&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">3、公司因合并、分立解散；&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">4、公司被依法责令关闭。 &nbsp;</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">二、公司注销的法律依据</span></strong></span></p></section></section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">根据《中华人民共和国公司法》第一百八十四条、第一百八十五条、第一百八十六条、第一百八十七条、第一百八十八条、第一百八十九条规定，注销公司依法依照如下步骤组织清算后，方能办理注销登记，公告终止公司。&nbsp;</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">&nbsp;<br/></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">1、依法成立清算组；&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2、公告并通知债权人申报债权，依法对债权进行登记；&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">3、清算组接管公司，展开清算工作；&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">4、清算组全面清理公司财产、编制资产负债表和财产清单；&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">5、清算组制定清算方案，并报股东会、股东大会或者人民法院确认；&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">6、根据股东会、股东大会或者人民法院确认的清算方案分配公司财产；&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">7、制作清算报告，报股东会、股东大会或者人民法院确认后，申请注销公司登记，公告公司终止。&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p><section><section><br/></section></section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">三、公司注销先税务后工商<br/></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">到税务局办理注销的企业，分为未领取加载统一社会信用代码营业执照（非一照一码纳税人）和已领取加载统一社会信用代码营业执照（一照一码纳税人）两种纳税人。</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">非一照一码纳税人：一定要带上税务登记证的正副本，带着公章到填写表格</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">一照一码纳税人：带好业执照的原件、复印件，带着公章填写表格。</span></p><section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">1、有结存发票（含所有发票）的纳税人，需要先在开票系统中作废未使用的发票，携带作废发票到发票窗口验旧缴销；若发票已经全部填开使用，也需要先到发票窗口验旧发票。</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2、使用金税盘或税控盘的纳税人在操作完上一步骤后，需要抄税（当月数据），然后填写《注销企业防伪税控设备登记表》，</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">3、综合窗口注销报税后，纳税人需要到信息中心注销金税盘或税控盘。</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">4、以上步骤操作完以后，准备注销前需要填写的各种表单，填写完毕以后到综合窗口办理：</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p></section></section></section></section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">（一）增值税申报表：</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">1、个体户：填写《增值税纳税申报表（小规模纳税人适用）》</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">填报说明：上季度已申报的只填写本季度的申报表即可；上季度未申报的需要填写上季度以及本季度的申报表。</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2、个体户一般纳税人：填写《增值税纳税申报表（一般纳税人适用）》</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">填报说明：上月份已申报的只填写本月份的申报表即可；上月份未申报的需要填写上月份以及本月份的申报表。</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">3、小规模纳税人企业：填写《增值税纳税申报表（小规模纳税人适用）》</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">填报说明：上季度已申报的只填写本季度的申报表即可；上季度未申报的需要填写上季度以及本季度的申报表；</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">4、一般纳税人企业：填写《增值税纳税申报表（一般纳税人适用）》</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">填报说明：上月份已申报的只填写本月份的申报表即可；上月份未申报的需要填写上月份以及本月份的申报表。</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">（二）企业所得税申报表</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">（2）纳税人存在未验旧的发票；</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">（3）土地增值税纳税人未完成土地增值税清算；</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">（4）企业所得税纳税人未完成企业所得税清算；</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">（5）存在未撤回出口退（免）税备案的；</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">（6）存在多缴（包括预缴、应退未退）税款；</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">（7）存在未结报的税收票证；</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; font-size: 16px; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(188, 37, 39); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">这5大税务问题，一定要提前处理好！&nbsp;</span></strong></span></p><section><section><section><section><br/></section></section></section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">1、印花税是注销必查项目</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">印花税作为一个小税种，平时在大家眼里无甚存在感！企业注销时，它就会让你尝尝忽视它的后果。</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">企业成立以来的重大合同，均会进行印花税审核，实收资本、资本公积、营业账簿、租赁、购销合同都是检查重点！</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">注销前，仔细检查一遍，该补的赶紧补！</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2、个人所得税也是个坑</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">某公司注销的时候，由于公司成立较早，公司注册资本的100万注册之后就以老板借款的名义出去了。</span></p><blockquote style=\"margin: 1em 0px; padding: 4px 0px 0px 10px; border-left: 3px solid rgb(219, 219, 219); color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.498); font-size: 15px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">&nbsp;财税[2003]158号规定：</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">个人投资者从其投资企业(个人独资企业、合伙企业除外)借款，在该纳税年度终了后既不归还，又未用于企业生产经营的，其未归还的借款可视为企业对个人投资者的红利分配，依照“利息、股息、红利所得”项目计征个人所得税。”</span></p></blockquote><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">因此，这家企业需要补缴个税：100*20%=20万元。</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">注销前一定要好好检查一下其他应收款！！！</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">3、账面存货要交税！</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">某一般纳税人企业，商贸批发行业，2017年年底，不想经营了，准备注销。但是账面还有10万元的存货，市场价（不含税）为12万元。税务上怎么处理呢？</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">一般纳税人终止生产经营，办理注销税务登记，要先办理一般纳税人注销，如果尚有未曾出售的存货，则会分配给股东或投资者，作为出资的收回或利润的分配。</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><blockquote style=\"margin: 1em 0px; padding: 4px 0px 0px 10px; border-left: 3px solid rgb(219, 219, 219); color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.498); font-size: 15px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">《增值税暂行条例实施细则》规定：</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">“将自产、委托加工或购买的货物分配给股东或投资者”属于视同销售行为。</span></p></blockquote><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">要按照12万确认销项，注销时，需缴纳增值税12*17%=2.04万元。</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">4、账面库存大于实物库存怎么处理？</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">通常，10家注销企业中有9家企业都存在这种问题！货物去哪儿了呢？肯定是有商品销售后漏报收入了！</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">比如说，A公司注销的时候，账面上有10万元的存货，市场价（不含税）为12万元，但实际上，仓库里面什么都没有了！税务实地核查发现这种情况，轻则按视同销售来处理，重则补缴滞纳金等！若按视同销售处理，则A公司需按照规定缴纳：12万*17%=2.04万元。</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">5、库存确实坏了咋办？</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">做食品销售的某公司，在注销的时候，公司仓库的117万元（含税）食品因管理不善，过期了，发票已经认证抵扣。</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">虽然账面上这117万元确实一分钱都不值了，但根据增值税管理办法，因管理不善造成损失，之前做了进项抵扣的必须进项转出。</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">进项转出金额=117/1.17*17%=17万元</span></p></section></section></section></section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">这几年国家政策越来越好，大力扶持中小型企业发展，也积极鼓励大众创业，所以这几年很多人都在开始去注册公司，有很多企业的发展也越来越兴旺，也有不少创业公司倒闭停止经营，大白不得不提醒那些不再经营的企业：<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">一旦不经营请尽快注销。</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><h2 class=\"\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-weight: 400; font-size: 16px; max-width: 100%; text-align: left; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; font-size: 16px; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(188, 37, 39); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">小公司不注销被税局罚款380万！</span></strong></span></h2><h2 class=\"\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-weight: 400; font-size: 16px; max-width: 100%; text-align: left; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; font-size: 16px; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(188, 37, 39); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">注销公司新规定出炉，工商与税务将实现信息共享！</span></strong></span></h2><section><section><section><section><br/></section></section></section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p></section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">据工商总局网站消息，工商总局、税务总局近日发布《关于加强信息共享和联合监管的通知》。通知要求协同推进企业简易注销登记改革，建立协同监管和信息共享机制，这将使企业注销登记更简易。<br/><br/><img src=\"/ueditor/php/upload/image/20190516/1557975332452240.jpg\" title=\"1557975332452240.jpg\" alt=\"005.jpg\" width=\"579\" height=\"317\"/></span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><section><section><section><section><section><section><section><section><section><section><section><section><section><section><span style=\"font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;;\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">一起因为注销引起的惨案，</span><span style=\"font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">前几年发生的一件事情的经过是这样的：</span></strong></span></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section><section><section><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.544px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.544px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">XX模具有限公司因行业变化，加上老板也有其他产业，所以决定不再经营了。公司老板就跟韩会计说，注销这家公司吧，公司太多麻烦！</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.544px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.544px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">韩会计心想，大家都说注销难，我可是熟门熟路了，之前办了几家有经验，应该是很顺利的啦！</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.544px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.544px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">于是，将注销资料交给税局一看，资产负债表中存货，还有原材料、库存商品830多万元。税务专管员没出声，说，你这资料还有点不齐，过几天齐了一起带来吧！</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.544px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br/></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.544px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; font-family: 微软雅黑, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">过了几天，突然税务稽查来了几个人，说要看看存货在哪里。当时韩会计就慌了，哪还有什么存货，那个数字就是挂的空账！</span></p><p style=\"margin-top: 0px;
